Focus

Disclaimer : The course was in Visual Code and multiple python files were created to make it more structured , since I am following along ,I have tried to implement everything in a single file. It should not be difficult to transform the code into more structured format akin to what it is in the course.

Content

import pandas as pd
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
res  = requests.get("https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_S&P_500_companies")
soup = BeautifulSoup(res.content,"html")
table = soup.find_all('table')
